Final state, once set, is immutable. This function may be called\n242:      * once or twice on a batch. It may be called twice if\n243:      * 1. An inflight batch expires before a response from the broker is received. The batch's final\n244:      * state is set to FAILED. But it could succeed on the broker and second time around batch.done() may\n245:      * try to set SUCCEEDED final state.\n246:      * 2. If a transaction abortion happens or if the producer is closed forcefully, the final state is\n247:      * ABORTED but again it could succeed if broker responds with a success.\n248:      *\n249:      * Attempted transitions from [FAILED | ABORTED] --> SUCCEEDED are logged.\n250:      * Attempted transitions from one failure state to the same or a different failed state are ignored.\n251:      * Attempted transitions from SUCCEEDED to the same or a failed state throw an exception.\n252:      *\n253:      * @param baseOffset The base offset of the messages assigned by the server\n254:      * @param logAppendTime The log append time or -1 if CreateTime is being used\n255:      * @param topLevelException The exception that occurred (or null if the request was successful)\n256:      * @param recordExceptions Record exception function mapping batchIndex to the respective record exception\n257:      * @return true if the batch was completed successfully and false if the batch was previously aborted\n258:      */\n259:     private boolean done(\n260:         long baseOffset,\n261:         long logAppendTime,\n262:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\n263:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions\n264:     ) {\n265:         final FinalState tryFinalState = (topLevelException == null) ? FinalState.SUCCEEDED : FinalState.FAILED;\n266:         if (tryFinalState == FinalState.SUCCEEDED) {\n267:             log.trace(\"Successfully produced messages to {} with base offset {}.\", topicPartition, baseOffset);\n268:         } else {\n269:             log.trace(\"Failed to produce messages to {} with base offset {}.\", topicPartition, baseOffset, topLevelException);\n270:         }\n271: \n272:         if (this.finalState.compareAndSet(null, tryFinalState)) {\n273:             completeFutureAndFireCallbacks(baseOffset, logAppendTime, recordExceptions);\n274:             return true;\n275:         }\n276: \n277:         if (this.finalState.get() != FinalState.SUCCEEDED) {\n278:             if (tryFinalState == FinalState.SUCCEEDED) {\n279:                 // Log if a previously unsuccessful batch succeeded later on.\n280:                 log.debug(\"ProduceResponse returned {} for {} after batch with base offset {} had already been {}.\",\n281:                     tryFinalState, topicPartition, baseOffset, this.finalState.get());\n282:             } else {\n283:                 // FAILED --> FAILED and ABORTED --> FAILED transitions are ignored.\n284:                 log.debug(\"Ignored state transition {} -> {} for {} batch with base offset {}\",\n285:                     this.finalState.get(), tryFinalState, topicPartition, baseOffset);\n286:             }\n287:         } else {\n288:             // A SUCCESSFUL batch must not attempt another state change.\n289:             throw new IllegalStateException(\"A \" + this.finalState.get() + \" batch must not attempt another state change to \" + tryFinalState);\n290:         }\n291:         return false;\n292:     }\n293: \n294:     private void completeFutureAndFireCallbacks(\n295:         long baseOffset,\n296:         long logAppendTime,\n297:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions\n298:     ) {\n299:         // Set the future before invoking the callbacks as we rely on its state for the `onCompletion` call\n300:         produceFuture.set(baseOffset, logAppendTime, recordExceptions);\n301: \n302:         // execute callbacks\n303:         for (int i = 0; i < null) {\n308:                         RecordMetadata metadata = thunk.future.value();\n309:                         thunk.callback.onCompletion(metadata, null);\n310:                     } else {\n311:                         RuntimeException exception = recordExceptions.apply(i);\n312:                         thunk.callback.onCompletion(null, exception);\n313:                     }\n314:                 }\n315:             } catch (Exception e) {\n316:                 log.error(\"Error executing user-provided callback on message for topic-partition '{}'\", topicPartition, e);\n317:             }\n318:         }\n319: \n320:         produceFuture.done();\n321:     }\n322: \n323:     public Deque<ProducerBatch> split(int splitBatchSize) {\n324:         RecordBatch recordBatch = \n348:     private Deque<ProducerBatch> splitRecordsIntoBatches(RecordBatch recordBatch, int splitBatchSize) {\n349:         Deque<ProducerBatch> batches = new ArrayDeque<>();\n350:         Iterator<Thunk> thunkIter = thunks.iterator();\n351:         // We always allocate batch size because we are already splitting a big batch.\n352:         // And we also Retain the create time of the original batch.\n353:         ProducerBatch batch = null;\n354: \n355:         for (Record record : recordBatch) {\n356:             assert thunkIter.hasNext();\n357:             Thunk thunk = batch.tryAppendForSplit(record.timestamp(), record.key(), record.value(), record.headers(), thunk);\n367:             }\n368:         }\n369: \n370:         // Close the last batch and add it to the batch list after split.\n371:         if (batch != null) {\n372:             batches.add(batch);\n373:             batch.closeForRecordAppends();\n374:         }\n375: \n376:         return has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\\n438:             // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\\n439:             // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\\n440:             pollTimeout = 0;\\n441:         }\\n442:         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\\n443:         return pollTimeout;\\n444:     }\\n445: \\n446:     /**\\n447:      * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\\n448:      */\\n449:     private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\\n450:         if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\\n451:             // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\\n452:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n453:             return true;\\n454:         }\\n455: \\n456:         if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) {\\n457:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(transactionManager.lastError());\\n458:         } else if (transactionManager.isAborting()) {\\n459:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\\n460:         }\\n461: \\n462:         TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\\n463:         if (nextRequestHandler == null)\\n464:             return false;\\n465: \\n466:         AbstractRequest.Builder<?> requestBuilder = nextRequestHandler.requestBuilder();\\n467:         Node targetNode = null;\\n468:         try {\\n469:             FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType = nextRequestHandler.coordinatorType();\\n470:             targetNode = coordinatorType != null ?\\n471:                     transactionManager.coordinator(coordinatorType) :\\n472:                     client.leastLoadedNode(time.milliseconds()).node();\\n473:             if (targetNode != null) {\\n474:                 if (!awaitNodeReady(targetNode, coordinatorType)) {\\n475:                     log.trace(\\\"Target node {} not ready within request timeout, will retry when node is ready.\\\", targetNode);\\n476:                     maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n477:                     return true;\\n478:                 }\\n479:             } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\\n480:                 log.trace(\\\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding coordinator.\\\", coordinatorType, requestBuilder.apiKey());\\n481:                 maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n482:                 return true;\\n483:             } else {\\n484:                 log.trace(\\\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\\\");\\n485:                 transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\\n486:                 client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n487:                 return true;\\n488:             }\\n489: \\n490:             if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\\n491:                 time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\\n492: \\n493:             long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\\n494:             ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\\n495:                 true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\\n496:             log.debug(\\\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\\\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\\n497:             client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n500:             return true;\\n501:         } catch (IOException e) {\\n502:             log.debug(\\\"Disconnect from {} while trying to send request {}. Going \\\" +\\n503:                     \\\"to back off and retry.\\\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\\n504:             // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\\n505:             maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n506:             return true;\\n507:         }\\n508:     }\\n509: \\n510:     private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\\n511:         if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\\n512:             transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\\n513:         } else {\\n514:             // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\\n515:             time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\\n516:             metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n517:         }\\n518: \\n519:         transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\\n520:     }\\n521: \\n522:     private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\\n523:         if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\\n524:             log.error(\\\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\\\", exception);\\n525:             accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\\n526:         }\\n527:     }\\n528: \\n529:     /**\\n530:      * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\\n531:      */\\n532:     public void initiateClose() {\\n533:         // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\\n534:         // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\\n535:         this.accumulator.close();\\n536:         this.running = false;\\n537:         this.wakeup();\\n538:     }\\n539: \\n540:     /**\\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\\n542:      */\\n543:     public void forceClose() {\\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\\n545:         initiateClose();\\n546:     }\\n547: \\n548:     public boolean isRunning() {\\n549:         return running;\\n550:     }\\n551: \\n552:     private boolean awaitNodeReady(Node node, FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType) throws IOException {\\n553:         if (NetworkClientUtils.awaitReady(client, node, time, requestTimeoutMs)) {\\n554:             if (coordinatorType == FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType.TRANSACTION) {\\n555:                 // Indicate to the transaction manager that the coordinator is ready, allowing it to check ApiVersions\\n556:                 // This allows us to bump transactional epochs even if the coordinator is temporarily unavailable at\\n557:                 // the time when the abortable error is \\n565:     /**\\n566:      * Handle a produce response\\n567:      */\\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\\n572:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\\\",\\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\\n574:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n575:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.REQUEST_TIMED_OUT, String.format(\\\"Disconnected from node %s due to timeout\\\", response.destination())),\\n576:                         correlationId, now, null);\\n577:         } else if (response.wasDisconnected()) {\\n578:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to node {} being disconnected\\\",\\n579:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\\n580:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n581:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NETWORK_EXCEPTION, String.format(\\\"Disconnected from node %s\\\", response.destination())),\\n582:                         correlationId, now, null);\\n583:         } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null)        for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\\n588:         } else {\\n589:             log.trace(\\\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\\\", response.destination(), correlationId);\\n590:             // if we have a response, parse it\\n591:             if (response.hasResponse()) {\\n592:                 // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\\n593:                 // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\\n595:                 // This will be set by completeBatch.\\n596:                 Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\\n604:                                 .stream()\\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\\n609: \\n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\\n614:                     TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\\n615:                             new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\\n617: \\n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\\n620:                         throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"Can't find batch created for topic id \\\" + r.topicId() +\\n621:                                 \\\" topic name \\\" + r.name() + \\\" partition \\\" + p.index() + \\\" using \\\" + topicNames);\\n622:                     }\\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\\n624:                 }));\\n625: \\n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\\n630:                         .collect(\\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\\\"For {} leader was updated.\\\", part)\\n636:                         );\\n637:                     }\\n638:                 }\\n639: \\n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\\n641:             } else {\\n642:                 // this is retry the given batch of records.\\n652:      *\\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\\n654:      * @param response The produce response\\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\\n658:      */\\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\\n662: \\n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\\n667:             log.warn(\\n668:                 \\\"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n669:                 correlationId,\\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\\n680:                 log.warn(\\n681:                     \\\"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n682:                     correlationId,\\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\\n691:                 //\\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\\n694:             } else {\\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\\n699:             }\\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\\n702:                     log.warn(\\\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \\\" +\\n703:                             \\\"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\\\",\\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\\n705:                 } else {\\n706:                     log.warn(\\\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \\\" +\\n707:                             \\\"to request metadata update now\\\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\\n708:                 }\\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\\n710:                     log.debug(\\\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\\\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\\n715:                     }\\n716:                 }\\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n718:             }\\n719:         } else {\\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\\n721:         }\\n722: \\n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\\n726:     }\\n727: \\n728:     /**\\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\\n730:      * e.g \\\"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\\\"\\n731:      */\\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\\n734:                 \\\"\\\" : String.format(\\\". Error Message: %s\\\", response.errorMessage);\\n735:         return String.format(\\\"%s%s\\\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\\n736:     }\\n737: \\n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n742:     }\\n743: \\n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\\n747:         }\\n748: \\n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n751:         }\\n752:     }\\n753: \\n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\\\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\\\");\\n762:         else\\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\\n764: \\n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n767:         } else {\\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\\n779:                 } else {\\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\\n781:                 }\\n782: \\n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\\n787:                 } else {\\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\\n789:                 }\\n790:             }\\n791: \\n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\\n795:                     return exception;\\n796:                 } else {\\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\\\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \\\" +\\n801:                         \\\"which had one more more invalid records\\\");\\n802:                 }\\n803:             };\\n804: \\n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n806:         }\\n807:     }\\n808: \\n809:     private void failBatch(\\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n813:     ) {\\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n815:     }\\n816: \\n817:     private void failBatch(\\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n822:     ) {\\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n824: \\n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\\n827:                 try {\\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\\n829:                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\\n830:                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n831:                 } catch (Exception e) {\\n832:                     log.debug(\\\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\\\", e);\\n833:                 }\\n834:             }\\n835:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n836:         }\\n837:     }\\n838: \\n839:     /**\\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\\n843:      */\\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\\n845:         return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\\n846:             batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\\n847:             !batch.isDone() &&\\n848:             (transactionManager == null ?\\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\\n851:     }\\n852: \\n853:     /**\\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\\n855:      */\\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\\n857:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\\n858:             sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\\n859:     }\\n860: \\n861:     /**\\n862:      * Create a produce request from the given record batches\\n863:      */\\n864:     private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n865:         if (batches.isEmpty())\\n866:             return;\\n867: \\n868:         final Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> recordsByPartition = new HashMap<>(batches.size());\\n869:         Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = topicIdsForBatches(batches);\\n870: \\n871:         ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection tpd = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection();\\n872:         for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\\n873:             TopicPartition tp = batch.topicPartition;\\n874:             MemoryRecords records = batch.records();\\n875:             Uuid topicId = topicIds.get(tp.topic());\\n876:             ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData tpData = tpd.find(tp.topic(), topicId);\\n877: \\n878:             if (tpData == null) {\\n879:                 tpData = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData()\\n880:                         .setTopicId(topicId).setName(tp.topic());\\n881:                 tpd.add(tpData);\\n882:             }\\n883: \\n884:             tpData.partitionData().add(new ProduceRequestData.PartitionProduceData()\\n885:                     .setIndex(tp.partition())\\n886:                     .setRecords(records));\\n887:             recordsByPartition.put(tp, batch);\\n888:         }\\n889: \\n890:         String transactionalId = null;\\n891:         boolean useTransactionV1Version = false;\\n892:         if (transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional()) {\\n893:             transactionalId = transactionManager.transactionalId();\\n894:             useTransactionV1Version = !transactionManager.isTransactionV2Enabled();\\n895:         }\\n896: \\n897:         ProduceRequest.Builder requestBuilder = ProduceRequest.builder(\\n898:                 new ProduceRequestData()\\n899:                         .setAcks(acks)\\n900:                         .setTimeoutMs(timeout)\\n901:                         .setTransactionalId(transactionalId)\\n902:                         .setTopicData(tpd),\\n903:                 useTransactionV1Version\\n904:         );\\n905:         // Fetch topic names from metadata outside callback as topic ids may change during the callback\\n906:         // for example if topic was recreated.\\n907:         Map<Uuid, String> topicNames = metadata.topicNames();\\n908: \\n909:         RequestCompletionHandler callback = response -> handleProduceResponse(response, recordsByPartition, topicNames, time.milliseconds());\\n910: \\n911:         String nodeId = Integer.toString(destination);\\n912:         ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(nodeId, requestBuilder, now, acks != 0,\\n913:                 requestTimeoutMs, callback);\\n914:         client.send(clientRequest, now);\\n915:         log.trace(\\\"Sent produce request to {}: {}\\\", nodeId, requestBuilder);\\n916:     }\\n917: \\n918:     private Map<String, Uuid> topicIdsForBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n919:         return batches.stream()\\n920:                 .collect(Collectors.toMap(\\n921:                         b -> b.topicPartition.topic(),\\n922:                         b -> metadata.topicIds().getOrDefault(b.topicPartition.topic(), Uuid.ZERO_UUID),\\n923:                         (existing, replacement) -> replacement)\\n924:                 );\\n925:     }\\n926: \\n927:     /**\\n928:      * Wake up the selector associated with this send thread\\n929:      */\\n930:     public void wakeup() {\\n931:         this.client.wakeup();\\n932:     }\\n933: \\n934:     public static Sensor throttleTimeSensor(SenderMetricsRegistry metrics) {\\n935:         Sensor produceThrottleTimeSensor = metrics.sensor(\\\"produce-throttle-time\\\");\\n936:         produceThrottleTimeSensor.add(metrics.produceThrottleTimeAvg, new Avg());\\n937:         produceThrottleTimeSensor.add(metrics.produceThrottleTimeMax, new Max());\\n938:         return produceThrottleTimeSensor;\\n939:     }\\n940: \\n941:     /**\\n942:      * A collection of sensors for the sender\\n943:      */\\n944:     private static class SenderMetrics {\\n945:         public       }\n226:     }\n227: \n228:     private boolean hasPendingTransactionalRequests() {\n229:         return transactionManager != null && transactionManager.hasPendingRequests() &&        log.debug(\"Starting Kafka producer I/O thread.\");\n238: \n239:         // main loop, runs until close is called\n240:         while (running) {\n241:             try {\n242: in the transaction manager, accumulator or waiting for acknowledgment,\n252:         // wait until these are completed.\n253:         while (!forceClose && ((this.accumulator.hasUndrained() || this.client.inFlightRequestCount() > 0) || hasPendingTransactionalRequests())) {\n254:             try {\n255:                 runOnce();\n256:             } catch (Exception e) {\n257:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n258:             }\n259:         }\n260: \n261:         // Abort the transaction if any commit or abort didn't go through the transaction manager's queue\n262:         while (!forceClose && transactionManager != null && transactionManager.hasOngoingTransaction()) {\n263:             if (!transactionManager.isCompleting()) {\n264:                 log.info(\"Aborting incomplete transaction due to shutdown\");\n265:                 try {\n266:                     // It is possible for the transaction manager to throw errors when aborting. Catch these\n267:                     // so as not to interfere with the rest of the shutdown logic.\n268:                     transactionManager.beginAbort();\n269:                 } catch (Exception e) {\n270:                     log.error(\"Error in kafka producer I/O thread while aborting transaction when during closing: \", e);\n271:                     // Force close in case the transactionManager is in error states.\n272:                     forceClose = true;\n273:                 }\n274:             }\n275:             try {\n276:                 runOnce();\n277:             } catch (Exception e) {\n278:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n279:             }\n280:         }\n281: \n282:         if (forceClose) {\n283:             // We need to fail all the incomplete transactional requests and batches and wake up the threads waiting on\n284:             // the futures.\n285:             if (transactionManager != null) {\n286:                 log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete transactional requests due to forced shutdown\");\n287:                 transactionManager.close();\n288:             }\n289:             log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete batches due to forced shutdown\");\n290:             this.accumulator.abortIncompleteBatches();\n291:         }\n292:         try {\n293:             this.client.close();\n294:         } catch (Exception e) {\n295:             log.error(\"Failed to close network client\", e);\n296:         }\n297: \n298:         log.debug(\"Shutdown of Kafka producer I/O thread has completed.\");\n299:     }\n300: \n301:     /**\n302:      * Run a single iteration of sending\n303:      *\n304:      */\n305:     void runOnce() {\n306:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n307:             try {\n308:                 transactionManager.maybeResolveSequences();\n309: \n310:                 RuntimeException lastError = transactionManager.lastError();\n311: \n312:                 // do not continue sending if the transaction manager is in a failed state\n313:                 if (transactionManager.hasFatalError()) {\n314:                     if (lastError != null)\n315:                         maybeAbortBatches(lastError);\n316:                     client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n317:                     return;\n318:                 }\n319: \n320:                 if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError() && shouldHandleAuthorizationError(lastError)) {\n321:                     return;\n322:                 }\n323: \n324:                 // Check whether we need a new producerId. If so, we will enqueue an InitProducerId\n325:                 // request which will be sent below\n326:                 transactionManager.bumpIdempotentEpochAndResetIdIfNeeded();\n327: \n328:                 if (maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest()) {\n329:                     return;\n330:                 }\n331:             } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n332:                 // This is already logged as error, but propagated here to perform any clean ups.\n333:                 log.trace(\"Authentication exception while processing transactional request\", e);\n334:                 transactionManager.authenticationFailed(e);\n335:             }\n336:         }\n337: \n338:         long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n339:         long pollTimeout = sendProducerData(currentTimeMs);\n340:         client.poll(pollTimeout, currentTimeMs);\n341:     }\n342: \n343:     // We handle {@code TransactionalIdAuthorizationException} and {@code ClusterAuthorizationException} by first\n344:     // failing the inflight requests, then transition the state to UNINITIALIZED so that the user doesn't need to\n345:     // instantiate the producer again.\n346:     private boolean shouldHandleAuthorizationError(RuntimeException exception) {\n347:         if (exception instanceof TransactionalIdAuthorizationException ||\n348:                         exception instanceof ClusterAuthorizationException) {\n349:             transactionManager.failPendingRequests(new AuthenticationException(exception));\n350:             maybeAbortBatches(exception);\n351:             transactionManager.transitionToUninitialized(exception);\n352:             return true;\n353:         }\n354:         return false;\n355:     }\n356: \n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\n359:         // get the list of partitions with data ready to send\n360:         RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);\n361: \n362:         // if there are any partitions whose leaders are not known yet, force metadata update\n363:         if (!result.unknownLeaderTopics.isEmpty()) {\n364:             // The set of topics with unknown leader contains topics with leader election pending as well as\n365:             // topics which may have expired. Add the topic again to metadata to ensure it is included\n366:             // and request metadata update, since there are messages to send to the topic.\n367:             for (String topic : result.unknownLeaderTopics)\n368:                 this.metadata.add(topic, now);\n369: \n370:             log.debug(\"Requesting metadata update due to unknown leader topics from the batched records: {}\",\n371:                 result.unknownLeaderTopics);\n372:             this.metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n373:         }\n374: \n375:         // remove any nodes we aren't ready to send to\n376:         Iterator<Node> iter = result.readyNodes.iterator();\n377:         long notReadyTimeout = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n378:         while (iter.hasNext()) {\n379:             Node node = iter.next();\n380:             if (!this.client.ready(node, now)) {\n381:                 // Update just the readyTimeMs of the latency stats, so that it moves forward\n382:                 // every time the batch is ready (then the difference between readyTimeMs and\n383:                 // drainTimeMs would represent how long data is waiting for the node).\n384:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, false);\n385:                 iter.remove();\n386:                 notReadyTimeout = Math.min(notReadyTimeout, this.client.pollDelayMs(node, now));\n387:             } else {\n388:                 // Update both readyTimeMs and drainTimeMs, this would \"reset\" the node\n389:                 // latency.\n390:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, true);\n391:             }\n392:         }\n393: \n394:         // create produce requests\n395:         Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\n396:         addToInflightBatches(batches);\n397:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder) {\n398:             // Mute all the partitions drained\n399:             for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\n400:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batchList)\n401:                     this.accumulator.mutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n402:             }\n403:         }\n404: \n405:         accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\n406:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\n407:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\n408:         expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n409: \n410:         // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\n411:         // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\n412:         // we need to reset the producer id here.\n413:         if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\n414:             log.trace(\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\", expiredBatches.size());\n415:         for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n416:             String errorMessage = \"Expiring \" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \" record(s) for \" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\n417:                 + \":\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \" ms has passed since batch creation\";\n418:             failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n419:             if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\n420:                 // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\n421:                 transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\n422:             }\n423:         }\n424:         sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\n425: \n426:         // If we have any nodes that are ready to send + have sendable data, poll with 0 timeout so this can immediately\n427:         // loop and try sending more data. Otherwise, the timeout will be the smaller value between next batch expiry\n428:         // time, and the delay time for checking data availability. Note that the nodes may have data that isn't yet\n429:         // sendable due to lingering, backing off, etc. This specifically does not include nodes with sendable data\n430:         // that aren't ready to send since they would cause busy looping.\n431:         long pollTimeout = Math.min(result.nextReadyCheckDelayMs, notReadyTimeout);\n432:         pollTimeout = Math.min(pollTimeout, this.accumulator.nextExpiryTimeMs() - now);\n433:         pollTimeout = Math.max(pollTimeout, 0);\n434:         if (!result.readyNodes.isEmpty()) {\n435:             log.trace(\"Nodes with data ready to send: {}\", result.readyNodes);\n436:             // if some partitions are already ready to be sent, the select time would be 0;\n437:             // otherwise if some partition already has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\n438:             // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\n439:             // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\n440:             pollTimeout = 0;\n441:         }\n442:         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\n443:         return pollTimeout;\n444:     }\n445: \n446:     /**\n447:      * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\n448:      */\n449:     private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\n450:         if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\n451:             // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\n452:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n453:             return true;\n454:         }\n455: \n456:         if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) {\n457:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(transactionManager.lastError());\n458:         } else if (transactionManager.isAborting()) {\n459:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\n460:         }\n461: \n462:         TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\n463:         if (nextRequestHandler == null)\n464:             return false;\n465: \n466:         AbstractRequest.Builder<?>          return true;\n478:                 }\n479:             } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\n480:                 log.trace(\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding coordinator.\", coordinatorType, requestBuilder.apiKey());\n481:                 maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n482:                 return true;\n483:             } else {\n484:                 log.trace(\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\");\n485:                 transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n486:                 client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n487:                 return true;\n488:             }\n489: \n490:             if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\n491:                 time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\n492: \n493:             long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n494:             ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\n495:                 true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\n496:             log.debug(\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\n497:             client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n500:             return true;\n501:         } catch (IOException e) {\n502:             log.debug(\"Disconnect from {} while trying to send request {}. Going \" +\n503:                     \"to back off and retry.\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\n504:             // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\n505:             maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n506:             return true;\n507:         }\n508:     }\n509: \n510:     private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\n511:         if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\n512:             transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\n513:         } else {\n514:             // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\n515:             time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\n516:             metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n517:         }\n518: \n519:         transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n520:     }\n521: \n522:     private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\n523:         if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\n524:             log.error(\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\", exception);\n525:             accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\n526:         }\n527:     }\n528: \n529:     /**\n530:      * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\n531:      */\n532:     public void initiateClose() {\n533:         // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\n534:         // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\n535:         this.accumulator.close();\n536:         this.running = false;\n537:         this.wakeup();\n538:     }\n539: \n540:     /**\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\n542:      */\n543:     public void forceClose() {\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\n545: /**\n566:      * Handle a produce response\n567:      */\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames,         log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\",\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\n574:             for (ProducerBatch partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\n604:                                 .stream()\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\n606:        new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\n617: \n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\n620: + topicNames);\n622:                     }\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\n624:                 }));\n625: \n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\n630:                         .collect(\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\n633:                     if  );\n637:                     }\n638:                 }\n639: \n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\n641:             } else {\n642: the given batch of records.\n652:      *\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\n654:      * @param response The produce response\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\n658:      */\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\n662: \n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\n667:             log.warn(\n668:                 \"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n669:                 correlationId,\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\n680:                 log.warn(\n681:                     \"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n682:                     correlationId,\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\n691:                 //\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\n694:             } else {\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\n699:             }\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\n702:                     log.warn(\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \" +\n703:                             \"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\",\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\n705:                 } else {\n706:                     log.warn(\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \" +\n707:                             \"to request metadata update now\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\n708:                 }\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\n710:                     log.debug(\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\n715:                     }\n716:                 }\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n718:             }\n719:         } else {\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\n721:         }\n722: \n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n726:     }\n727: \n728:     /**\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\n730:      * e.g \"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\"\n731:      */\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\n734:                 \"\" : String.format(\". Error Message: %s\", response.errorMessage);\n735:         return String.format(\"%s%s\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\n736:     }\n737: \n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n742:     }\n743: \n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\n747:         }\n748: \n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n751:         }\n752:     }\n753: \n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\");\n762:         else\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\n764: \n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n767:         } else {\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\n779:                 } else {\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\n781:                 }\n782: \n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\n787:                 } else {\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\n789:                 }\n790:             }\n791: \n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\n795:                     return exception;\n796:                 } else {\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \" +\n801:                         \"which had one more more invalid records\");\n802:                 }\n803:             };\n804: \n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n806:         }\n807:     }\n808: \n809:     private void failBatch(\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n813:     ) {\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n815:     }\n816: \n817:     private void failBatch(\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n822:     ) {\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n824: \n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\n827:                 try {\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\n829:                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\n830:                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n831:                 } catch (Exception e) {\n832:                     log.debug(\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\", e);\n833:                 }\n834:             }\n835:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n836:         }\n837:     }\n838: \n839:     /**\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\n843:      */\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\n845:         return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\n846:             batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\n847:             !batch.isDone() &&\n848:             (transactionManager == null ?\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\n851:     }\n852: \n853:     /**\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\n855:      */\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\n857:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\n858:             sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\n859:     }\n860: \n861:     /**\n862:      * Create a produce request from the given record batches\n863:      */\n864:     private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n865:         if (batches.isEmpty())\n866:             return;\n867: \n868:         final Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> recordsByPartition = new HashMap<>(batches.size());\n869:         Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = topicIdsForBatches(batches);\n870: \n871:         ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection tpd = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection();\n872:         for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\n873:             TopicPartition tp = batch.topicPartition;\n874:             MemoryRecords records = batch.records();\n875:             Uuid topicId = topicIds.get(tp.topic());\n876:             ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData tpData = tpd.find(tp.topic(), topicId);\n877: \n878:             if (tpData == null) {\n879:                 tpData = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData()\n880:                         .setTopicId(topicId).setName(tp.topic());\n881:                 tpd.add(tpData);\n882:             }\n883: \n884:             tpData.partitionData().add(new ProduceRequestData.PartitionProduceData()\n885:                     .setIndex(tp.partition())\n886:                     .setRecords(records));\n887:             recordsByPartition.put(tp, batch);\n888:         }\n889: \n890:         String transactionalId = null;\n891:         boolean useTransactionV1Version = false;\n892:         if (transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional()) {\n893:             transactionalId = transactionManager.transactionalId();\n894:             useTransactionV1Version = !transactionManager.isTransactionV2Enabled();\n895:         }\n896: \n897:         ProduceRequest.Builder requestBuilder = ProduceRequest.builder(\n898:                 new ProduceRequestData()\n899:
